Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111 Enforcement of environmental covenant.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1): A civil action for injunctive or other equitable relief for violation of an environmental covenant may be maintained by:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1)(a): a party to the covenant;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1)(b): the agency;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1)(c): any person to whom the covenant expressly grants power to enforce;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1)(d): a person whose interest in the real property or whose collateral or liability may be affected by the alleged violation of the covenant; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(1)(e): a municipality or other unit of local government in which the real property subject to the covenant is located.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(2): This chapter does not limit the regulatory authority of the agency under law other than this chapter with respect to an environmental response project.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(3): A person is not responsible for or subject to liability for environmental remediation solely because the person has the right to enforce an environmental covenant.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-111(4): (1) In addition to Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-112 Uniformity of application and construction.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
In applying and construing this chapter, consideration must be given to the need to promote uniformity of the law with respect to its subject matter among jurisdictions that enact it.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-113 Relation to Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
This chapter modifies, limits, or supersedes the federal Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act, 15 U.S.C. Section 7001 et seq., but does not modify, limit, or supersede Section 101 of that Act, 15 U.S.C. Section 7001(a), or authorize electronic delivery of any of the notices described in Section 103 of that Act, 15 U.S.C. Section 7003(b).

Utah Code Annotated § 57-25-114 Severability.
---------------------------------------------
If any provision of this chapter or its application to any person or circumstance is held invalid, the invalidity does not affect other provisions or applications of this chapter that can be given effect without the invalid provision or application, and to this end the provisions of this chapter are severable.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 57 - Chapter 26 - Utah Uniform Assignment of Rents Act
**********************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
This chapter is known as the "Utah Uniform Assignment of Rents Act."

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(1): "Assignee" means a person entitled to enforce an assignment of rents.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(2): "Assignment of rents" means a transfer of an interest in rents in connection with an obligation secured by real property located in this state and from which the rents arise.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(3): "Assignor" means a person that makes an assignment of rents or the successor owner of the real property from which the rents arise.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(4): "Cash proceeds" means proceeds that are money, checks, deposit accounts, or the like.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(5): "Day" means calendar day.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(6): "Deposit account" means a demand, time, savings, passbook, or similar account maintained with a bank, savings bank, savings and loan association, credit union, or trust company.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(7): "Document" means information that is inscribed on a tangible medium or that is stored on an electronic or other medium and is retrievable in perceivable form.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(8): "Notification" means a document containing information that this chapter requires a person to provide to another, signed by the person required to provide the information.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(9): "Person" means an individual, corporation, business trust, estate, trust, partnership, limited liability company, association, joint venture, public corporation, government, or governmental subdivision, agency, or instrumentality, or any other legal or commercial entity.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(10): "Proceeds" means personal property that is received or collected on account of a tenant's obligation to pay rents.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(11): "Purchase" means to take by sale, lease, discount, negotiation, mortgage, pledge, trust deed, lien, security interest, issue or reissue, gift, or any other voluntary transaction creating an interest in property.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12): "Rents" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(a): sums payable for the right to possess or occupy, or for the actual possession or occupation of, real property of another person;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(b): sums payable to an assignor under a policy of rental interruption insurance covering real property;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(c): claims arising out of a default in the payment of sums payable for the right to possess or occupy real property of another person;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(d): sums payable to terminate an agreement to possess or occupy real property of another person;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(e): sums payable to an assignor for payment or reimbursement of expenses incurred in owning, operating and maintaining, or constructing or installing improvements on, real property; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(12)(f): any other sums payable under an agreement relating to the real property of another person that constitute rents under law of this state other than this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(13): "Secured obligation" means an obligation the performance of which is secured by an assignment of rents.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(14): "Security instrument" means a document, however denominated, that creates or provides for a security interest in real property, whether or not it also creates or provides for a security interest in personal property.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(15): "Security interest" means an interest in property that arises by agreement and secures performance of an obligation.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(16): "Sign" means, with present intent to authenticate or adopt a document:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(16)(a): to execute or adopt a tangible symbol; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(16)(b): to attach to or logically associate with the document an electronic sound, symbol, or process.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(17): "State" means a state of the United States, the District of Columbia, Puerto Rico, the United States Virgin Islands, or any territory or insular possession subject to the jurisdiction of the United States.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(18): Title 57, Chapter 3, Recording of Documents "Submit for recording" means to submit a document complying with applicable legal standards, with required fees and taxes, to the appropriate governmental office under
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-102(19): "Tenant" means a person that has an obligation to pay sums for the right to possess or occupy, or for possessing or occupying, the real property of another person.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103 Manner of giving notification.
--------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(1): (3); (4); (2) Except as otherwise provided in Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(1)(a): (2) by depositing it with the United States Postal Service or with a commercially reasonable delivery service, properly addressed to the intended recipient's address as specified in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(1)(b): if the recipient agreed to receive notification by facsimile transmission, electronic mail, or other electronic transmission, by sending it to the recipient in the agreed manner at the address specified in the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(2): (1) The following rules determine the proper address for giving a notification under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(2)(a): A person giving a notification to an assignee shall use the address for notices to the assignee provided in the document creating the assignment of rents, but, if the assignee has provided the person giving the notification with a more recent address for notices, the person giving the notification shall use that address.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(2)(b): A person giving a notification to an assignor shall use the address for notices to the assignor provided in the document creating the assignment of rents, but, if the assignor has provided the person giving the notification with a more recent address for notices, the person giving the notification shall use that address.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(2)(c): If a tenant's agreement with an assignor provides an address for notices to the tenant and the person giving notification has received a copy of the agreement or knows the address for notices specified in the agreement, the person giving the notification shall use that address in giving a notification to the tenant.  Otherwise, the person shall use the address of the premises covered by the agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(3): If a person giving a notification pursuant to this chapter and the recipient have agreed to the method for giving a notification, any notification must be given by that method.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-103(4): (1); (3) If a notification is received by the recipient, it is effective even if it was not given in accordance with Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-104 Security instrument creates assignment of rents -- Assignment of rents creates security interest.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-104(1): An enforceable security instrument creates an assignment of rents arising from the real property described in the security instrument, unless the security instrument provides otherwise.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-104(2): An assignment of rents creates a presently effective security interest in all accrued and unaccrued rents arising from the real property described in the document creating the assignment, regardless of whether the document is in the form of an absolute assignment, an absolute assignment conditioned upon default, an assignment as additional security, or any other form.  The security interest in rents is separate and distinct from any security interest held by the assignee in the real property.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105 Recordation -- Perfection of security interest in rents -- Priority of conflicting interests in rents.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(1): A document creating an assignment of rents may be submitted for recording in the office of the county recorder for the county in which the property is situated in the same manner as any other document evidencing a conveyance of an interest in real property.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(2): Upon recording, the security interest in rents created by an assignment of rents is fully perfected, even if a provision of the document creating the assignment or law of this state other than this chapter would preclude or defer enforcement of the security interest until the occurrence of a subsequent event, including a subsequent default of the assignor, the assignee's obtaining possession of the real property, or the appointment of a receiver.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(3): (4) Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(3)(a): acquires a judicial lien against the rents or the real property from which the rents arise; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(3)(b): purchases an interest in the rents or the real property from which the rents arise.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-105(4): (3) A perfected security interest in rents has priority over the rights of a person described in Subsection


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-106 Enforcement of security interest in rents.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-106(1): 57-26-107; 57-26-108; 57-26-109 An assignee may enforce an assignment of rents using one or more of the methods specified in Sections
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-106(2): 57-26-107 From the date of enforcement, the assignee or, in the case of enforcement by appointment of a receiver under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-106(2)(a): have accrued but remain unpaid on that date; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-106(2)(b): accrue on or after that date, as those rents accrue.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107 Enforcement by appointment of receiver.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1): An assignee is entitled to the appointment of a receiver for the real property subject to the assignment of rents if:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(a): the assignor is in default and:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(a)(i): the assignor has agreed in a signed document to the appointment of a receiver in the event of the assignor's default;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(a)(ii): it appears likely that the real property may not be sufficient to satisfy the secured obligation;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(a)(iii): the assignor has failed to turn over to the assignee proceeds that the assignee was entitled to collect; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(a)(iv): a subordinate assignee of rents obtains the appointment of a receiver for the real property; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(1)(b): other circumstances exist that would justify the appointment of a receiver under law of this state other than this chapter.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(2): An assignee may file a petition for the appointment of a receiver in connection with an action:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(2)(a): to foreclose the security instrument;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(2)(b): for specific performance of the assignment;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(2)(c): seeking a remedy on account of waste or threatened waste of the real property subject to the assignment; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(2)(d): otherwise to enforce the secured obligation or the assignee's remedies arising from the assignment.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(3): (2); 57-26-103 An assignee that files a petition under Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(4): If an assignee enforces an assignment of rents under this section, the date of enforcement is the date on which the court enters an order appointing a receiver for the real property subject to the assignment.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(5): 57-26-106(2) From the date of its appointment, a receiver is entitled to collect rents as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(6): The following rules govern priority among receivers:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(6)(a): If more than one assignee qualifies under this section for the appointment of a receiver, a receivership requested by an assignee entitled to priority in rents under this chapter has priority over a receivership requested by a subordinate assignee, even if a court has previously appointed a receiver for the subordinate assignee.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-107(6)(b): If a subordinate assignee obtains the appointment of a receiver, the receiver may collect the rents and apply the proceeds in the manner specified in the order appointing the receiver until a receiver is appointed under a senior assignment of rents.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-108 Enforcement by notification to assignor.
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-108(1): 57-26-106 Upon the assignor's default, or as otherwise agreed by the assignor, the assignee may give the assignor a notification demanding that the assignor pay over the proceeds of any rents that the assignee is entitled to collect under Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-108(2): (1) If an assignee enforces an assignment of rents under this section, the date of enforcement is the date on which the assignor receives a notification under Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109 Enforcement by notification to tenant.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1): (3); (4) Upon the assignor's default, or as otherwise agreed by the assignor, the assignee may give to a tenant of the real property a notification demanding that the tenant pay to the assignee all unpaid accrued rents and all unaccrued rents as they accrue.  The assignee shall give a copy of the notification to the assignor and to any other person that, 10 days before the notification date, held a recorded assignment of rents arising from the real property.  The notification must be signed by the assignee and:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(a): identify the tenant, assignor, assignee, premises covered by the agreement between the tenant and the assignor, and assignment of rents being enforced;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(b): provide the recording data for the document creating the assignment or other reasonable proof that the assignment was made;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(c): state that the assignee has the right to collect rents in accordance with the assignment;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(d): direct the tenant to pay to the assignee all unpaid accrued rents and all unaccrued rents as they accrue;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(e): (3); (4) describe the manner in which Subsections
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(f): provide the name and telephone number of a contact person and an address to which the tenant can direct payment of rents and any inquiry for additional information about the assignment or the assignee's right to enforce the assignment; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(1)(g): contain a statement that the tenant may consult a lawyer if the tenant has questions about its rights and obligations.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(2): (1) If an assignee enforces an assignment of rents under this section, the date of enforcement is the date on which the tenant receives a notification substantially complying with Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-109(3): (4); (1) Subject to Subsection

Unless otherwise agreed, an assignee that collects rents under this chapter or collects upon a judgment in an action under SubsectionUtah Code Annotated § 57-26-112(1): the assignee's reasonable expenses of enforcing its assignment of rents, including, to the extent provided for by agreement and not prohibited by law of this state other than this chapter, reasonable attorney fees and costs incurred by the assignee;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-112(2): reimbursement of any expenses incurred by the assignee to protect or maintain the real property subject to the assignment;

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-112(5): the assignor.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-113 Application of proceeds to expenses of protecting real property -- Claims and defenses of tenant.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-113(3): This chapter does not limit the standing or right of a tenant to request a court to appoint a receiver for the real property subject to the assignment or to seek other relief on the ground that the assignee's nonpayment of expenses of protecting or maintaining the real property has caused or threatened harm to the tenant's interest in the property.  Whether the tenant is entitled to the appointment of a receiver or other relief is governed by law of this state other than this chapter.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-114(2)(b): the assignee continues to have a security interest in the proceeds so long as they are identifiable.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-114(3): For purposes of this chapter, cash proceeds are identifiable if they are maintained in a segregated account or, if commingled with other funds, to the extent the assignee can identify them by a method of tracing, including application of equitable principles, that is permitted under law of this state other than this chapter with respect to commingled funds.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-114(4): (2); (2) In addition to any other remedy available to the assignee under law of this state other than this chapter, if an assignor fails to turn over proceeds to the assignee as required by Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115 Perfection and priority of assignee's security interest in proceeds.
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(1): Title 70A, Chapter 9a, Uniform Commercial Code - Secured Transactions; Title 70A, Chapter 9a, Uniform Commercial Code - Secured Transactions In this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(1)(a): Title 70A, Chapter 9a, Uniform Commercial Code - Secured Transactions; Title 70A, Chapter 9a, Uniform Commercial Code - Secured Transactions "Article 9" means
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(1)(b): "Conflicting interest" means an interest in proceeds, held by a person other than an assignee, that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(1)(b)(i): a security interest arising under Article 9; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(1)(b)(ii): any other interest if Article 9 resolves the priority conflict between that person and a secured party with a conflicting security interest in the proceeds.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(2): An assignee's security interest in identifiable cash proceeds is perfected if its security interest in rents is perfected.  An assignee's security interest in identifiable noncash proceeds is perfected only if the assignee perfects that interest in accordance with Article 9.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(3): (4) Except as otherwise provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(4): An assignee's perfected security interest in identifiable cash proceeds is subordinate to a conflicting interest that is perfected by control under Article 9 but has priority over a conflicting interest that is perfected other than by control.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-115(5): An assignee's perfected security interest in identifiable cash proceeds is subordinate to a conflicting interest arising under a right of recoupment or setoff.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-116 Priority subject to subordination.
------------------------------------------------------------------
This chapter does not preclude subordination by agreement as to rents or proceeds.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-117 Uniformity of application and construction.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------
In applying and construing this uniform act, consideration must be given to the need to promote uniformity of the law with respect to its subject matter among states that enact it.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-118 Relation to Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act.
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
This chapter modifies, limits, and supersedes the federal Electronic Signatures in Global and National Commerce Act (15 U.S.C. Section 7001, et seq.) but does not modify, limit, or supersede Section 101(c) of that act (15 U.S.C. Section 7001(c)) or authorize electronic delivery of any of the notices described in Section 103(b) of that act (15 U.S.C. Section 7003(b)).

Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119 Application to existing relationships.
----------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(1): Except as otherwise provided in this section, this chapter governs the enforcement of an assignment of rents and the perfection and priority of a security interest in rents, even if the document creating the assignment was signed and delivered before May 12, 2009.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(2): This chapter does not affect an action or proceeding commenced before May 12, 2009.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(3): 57-26-104(1) Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(4): This chapter does not affect:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(4)(a): the enforceability of an assignee's security interest in rents or proceeds if, immediately before May 12, 2009, that security interest was enforceable;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(4)(b): the perfection of an assignee's security interest in rents or proceeds if, immediately before May 12, 2009, that security interest was perfected; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-26-119(4)(c): the priority of an assignee's security interest in rents or proceeds with respect to the interest of another person if, immediately before May 12, 2009, the interest of the other person was enforceable and perfected, and that priority was established.

Utah Code Annotated - Title 57 - Chapter 28 - Utah Reverse Mortgage Act
***********************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-101(1): This chapter is known as the "Utah Reverse Mortgage Act."
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-101(2): This part is known as "General Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(1): "Borrower" means an individual who executes an agreement for a reverse mortgage.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(2): "Dwelling" means:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(2)(a): a one- to four-family residence in which the borrower occupies at least one unit;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(2)(b): a condominium project approved by the United States Department of Housing and Urban Development; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(2)(c): a manufactured home built after June 1976.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(3): "Independent housing counselor" means a person who is listed on the United States Department of Housing and Urban Development's Home Equity Conversion Mortgage Counselor Roster described in 24 C.F.R. Part 206.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(4): "Lender" means a person who makes a reverse mortgage.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(5): "Line of credit payment option" means a loan disbursement plan for a reverse mortgage under which the lender pays the loan proceeds to the borrower at times and in amounts determined by the borrower.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(6): "Means-tested program of aid to individuals" means any law or program that relates to payments, allowances, benefits, or services that are provided on a means-tested basis by the state.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(7): "Principal residence" means the dwelling:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(7)(a): that an individual maintains as the individual's permanent place of abode; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(7)(b): where the individual typically spends the majority of the calendar year.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8): "Reverse mortgage" means a nonrecourse loan that:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(a): is secured by the borrower's principal residence;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(b): provides cash advances to the borrower based on the borrower's equity in the borrower's principal residence; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c): does not require payment of principal or interest until:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(i): each borrower dies;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(ii): the borrower's principal residence is transferred;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(iii): the dwelling that secures the loan is no longer the borrower's principal residence;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(iv): 
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(iv)(A): the borrower fails to occupy the property that secures the loan for more than 12 months because of physical or mental illness; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(iv)(B): no other borrower maintains the property as a principal residence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(8)(c)(v): the borrower defaults.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(9): "Tenure payment option" means a loan disbursement plan for a reverse mortgage under which the lender pays the loan proceeds to the borrower in equal monthly installments for as long as the dwelling that secures the reverse mortgage remains the borrower's principal residence.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-102(10): "Term payment option" means a loan disbursement plan for a reverse mortgage under which the lender pays the loan proceeds to the borrower in equal monthly installments for a fixed term that is chosen by the lender.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-201 Title.
--------------------------------------
This part is known as "Reverse Mortgage Requirements."

Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-202 Borrower requirements.
------------------------------------------------------
A borrower shall:Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-202(1): 
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-202(1)(a): for a home equity conversion mortgage insured by the Federal Housing Administration under
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-202(1)(b): for proprietary loans not insured by the Federal Housing Administration, be 55 years old or older; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-202(2): occupy the dwelling that secures the reverse mortgage as a principal residence.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203 Disclosures to borrower.
--------------------------------------------------------
A lender shall give a prospective borrower or a borrower the following written disclosures:Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1): at the time the lender provides an application for a reverse mortgage to a prospective borrower:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1)(a): a disclosure that explains any adjustable interest rate feature of the reverse mortgage, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1)(a)(i): the circumstances under which the interest rate may increase;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1)(a)(ii): any limitation on the amount that the interest rate may increase; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1)(a)(iii): the effect of an increase in the interest rate; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(1)(b): a list of at least five independent housing counselors that includes each independent housing counselor's name, address, and telephone number;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2): at least 10 days before the day on which a reverse mortgage closes, a disclosure that describes:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2)(a): that the prospective borrower's liability under the reverse mortgage is limited;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2)(b): the prospective borrower's rights, obligations, and remedies that relate to:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2)(b)(i): temporary absences, late payments, and payment default by the lender; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2)(b)(ii): each condition that requires satisfaction of the reverse mortgage; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(2)(c): the projected total cost of the reverse mortgage to the prospective borrower, based on the projected total future loan balance;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(3): on an annual basis, on or before January 31 of each year, a statement that summarizes:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(3)(a): the total principal amount paid to the borrower under the reverse mortgage;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(3)(b): the total amount of deferred interest added to the principal; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(3)(c): the outstanding loan balance at the end of the preceding year; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(4): if applicable, at least 25 days before the day on which the lender adjusts the interest rate on a reverse mortgage, a disclosure that states:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(4)(a): the current index amount;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(4)(b): the publication date of the index; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-203(4)(c): the new interest rate.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-204 Independent counseling.
-------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-204(1): 57-28-202(1)(a); 57-28-202(1)(b) As used in this section:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-204(1)(a): 57-28-202(1)(a) "Federally insured loan borrower" means a borrower described in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-204(1)(b): 57-28-202(1)(b) "Non-federally insured loan borrower" means a borrower described in Subsection

Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205 Costs and repayment.
----------------------------------------------------
A lender may collect the following charges and fees in connection with the origination of a reverse mortgage:Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(1): the actual expenses that the lender incurs in originating and closing the reverse mortgage, including a mortgage broker's fee if the mortgage broker and the lender do not share any pecuniary interests; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2): the actual amount that the lender paid for:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(a): a recording fee;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(b): a credit report;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(c): a survey, if required by the lender or the borrower;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(d): a title examination;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(e): the lender's title insurance; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-205(2)(f): an initial appraisal of the real property that secures the reverse mortgage.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-28-302 Treatment of loan proceeds -- Effect on assistance eligibility.
-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

***********************************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-101 Title.
--------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-101(1): This chapter is known as the "Undivided Fractionalized Long-Term Estate Sales Practices Act."
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-101(2): This part is known as "General Provisions."


Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(1): 61-2f-103 "Commission" means the Real Estate Commission created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(2): "Director" means the director of the Division of Real Estate.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(3): 61-2-201 "Division" means the Division of Real Estate created in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(4): "Management agreement" means an agreement between a person and each owner of an undivided fractionalized long-term estate in a piece of real property under which the person agrees to manage the leasing or operations of the real property.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(5): "Master lease" means an agreement under which a person is granted a leasehold interest in real property and may sublease all or a portion of the real property to one or more persons.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(6): "Master lease tenant" means the lessee in a master lease.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(7): "Sponsor" means a person who is the original seller of an undivided fractionalized long-term estate.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(8): 
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(8)(a): "Undivided fractionalized long-term estate" means an ownership interest in real property by two or more persons that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(8)(a)(i): a tenancy in common; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(8)(a)(ii): a fee estate.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-102(8)(b): "Undivided fractionalized long-term estate" does not include a joint tenancy.

Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303 Investigatory powers and proceedings of division.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(1): The division may:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(1)(a): conduct a public or private investigation to determine whether a person has violated or is about to violate a provision of this chapter; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(1)(b): require or allow a person to file a written statement with the division that relates to the facts and circumstances concerning a matter to be investigated.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2): For the purpose of an investigation or proceeding under this chapter, the division may:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(a): administer oaths or affirmations; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b): upon the division's own initiative or upon the request of any party:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(i): subpoena a witness;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(ii): compel a witness's attendance;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(iii): take evidence; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(iv): require the production, within 10 business days, of any information or item that is relevant to the investigation, including:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(iv)(A): the existence, description, nature, custody, condition, and location of any books, electronic records, documents, or other tangible records;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(iv)(B): the identity and location of any person who has knowledge of relevant facts; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(2)(b)(iv)(C): any other information or item that is reasonably calculated to lead to the discovery of material evidence.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(3): If a person fails to obey a subpoena or other request made in accordance with this section, the division may file an action in district court for an order compelling compliance.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303 Investigatory powers and proceedings of division.
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-29-303(1): The division may:

Utah Code Annotated - Title 57 - Chapter 30 - Residential Property Service Agreements
*************************************************************************************

Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101 Definitions.
--------------------------------------------
As used in this chapter:Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(1): 57-25-102 "Common interest community" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(2): 31A-6a-101 "Home warranty service contract" means the same as that term is defined in Section
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(3): "Record" means to submit a document to a county recorder for official placement in a public land record.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4): (4)(b)
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(a): (4)(b) "Residential property service agreement" means, except as provided in Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(a)(i): the purchase or sale of residential real estate; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(a)(ii): the maintenance of residential real estate in preparation for purchase or sale.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b): "Residential property service agreement" does not include:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b)(i): a home warranty service agreement;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b)(ii): an insurance contract;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b)(iii): an agreement for an option to purchase or right of refusal;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b)(iv): a maintenance or repair agreement between an owner of real property within a common interest community and a homeowners' association or other similar organization; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(4)(b)(v): an agreement to provide Internet or utility equipment or services.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(5): "Residential real estate" means real property located in the state that is:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(5)(a): used primarily for a personal, family, or household purpose; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-101(5)(b): contains fewer than five dwelling units.


Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201 Prohibited residential property service agreements -- Recording -- Damages -- Actual or constructive notice.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1): (1)(a)
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a): A residential property service agreement entered into after May 3, 2023, may not:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(i): allow the services to be provided under the agreement to begin more than one year after the day on which the residential property service agreement is signed by all parties;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(ii): indicate that the residential property service agreement:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(ii)(A): runs with the land;
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(ii)(B): is binding on a future owner of an interest in the residential real estate that is the subject of the residential property service agreement; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(ii)(C): creates a lien, encumbrance, or other real property security interest; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(a)(iii): allow for the assignment of the right to provide the services without notice to and agreement by the owner of the residential real estate that is the subject of the residential property service agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(b): (1)(a) A residential property service agreement that violates Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(b)(i): is void; and
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(1)(b)(ii): does not provide actual or constructive notice to a bona fide purchaser or creditor.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2): (2)(a); (2)(a); (2)(a); Title 38, Chapter 9, Wrongful Lien Act
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2)(a): A person may not record or cause to be recorded:
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2)(a)(i): a void residential property service agreement; or
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2)(a)(ii): a notice or memorandum concerning a void residential property service agreement.
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2)(b): (2)(a); (2)(a) If a document is recorded in violation of Subsection
Utah Code Annotated § 57-30-201(2)(c): (2)(a); Title 38, Chapter 9, Wrongful Lien Act A document recorded in violation of Subsection
